On Insulting Others and Self-Insult (II)

Only self-insult invites insult. Having discussed this yesterday, I would like to discuss it further. If one is insulted by others for no reason, the blame and shame lie with the insulter. If a butcher is suddenly attacked by a robber who binds his hands and feet and empties his pockets, the butcher certainly suffers, but it is not the butcher's shame. The violent criminal who robs for gain and defies righteousness is truly shameful and truly an enemy of mankind. If there is any justice in the world, the occurrence of such violence is a shame to all mankind. The actions that defy public reason and justice are seen by all, and cannot escape the final judgment of public reason and justice. Therefore, after the Wanbaoshan Incident, the Japanese forced the Koreans to boycott the Chinese, and massacres of Chinese occurred in various parts of Korea. Our people have already understood the hidden motives, and the clear-eyed Koreans have repeatedly revealed their conspiracy and expressed their apologies to us. When the thugs attacked the Chinese street in Incheon with great momentum and extreme danger, the British consul came forward to uphold justice. The Japanese cruelty and wickedness were further revealed to the world, and it is even more evident that behavior that defies public reason is abandoned by all mankind. Pointed at by thousands, one dies without disease. The previous Germany is an example. We only need to look at the crab with disdain, seeing how long it can move sideways. Suffering persecution is not a cause for much worry. Only self-insult cultivates it gradually, accumulates it subtly. Accumulation makes it irreversible. Self-insult without realizing it eventually develops into an irreparable crisis. Being self-important and self-enclosed is self-insult. Comfort and ease, extravagance and indulgence are self-insult. The rampant spread of bandits and the frequent occurrence of famines are self-insult. Having our own minerals but not being able to develop them, having our own land but not being able to cultivate it, is self-insult. The initiative of being insulted lies with others, the initiative of self-insult lies with ourselves. Being insulted is obvious, self-insult gradually becomes imperceptible. Its shame is a hundred times, a thousand times greater than being insulted. This is truly the national and ethnic humiliation of our country. In the past hundred years, the people of our country have been singing and dancing merrily in this national and ethnic humiliation, feeling content and not blushing at the mockery of other countries. Once foreign insult arrives, they cry out to public reason and justice and declare to other countries: "This is our shame!" Few are spared from being ridiculed, and nothing could be more worthy of tears than this. Although being insulted and self-insult are both insults, being conquered and self-destruction are both destruction, but foreign insult can still be avenged, while self-insult cannot be avenged. Foreign conquest can still be saved, while self-destruction cannot be saved. Therefore, when faced with the influx of foreign insults, the people of our country should resist foreign insults with a united spirit, and even more so, they should no longer engage in self-insult with a united spirit. Otherwise, we truly have nothing to say about the vast future. The arrival of foreign insults is not limited to the current situation.

Wang Jia-zhen Discusses His Departure Date for Europe

Ministry of Industry Cracks Down on Japanese Fishing Vessels

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry believes that Japanese fishing vessels have repeatedly violated the sea to fish, but the prohibition has not been implemented. Now, large numbers of Japanese fishing vessels are arbitrarily invading our territorial waters, which hinders our sovereignty. Therefore, measures to crack down on them are proposed: (1) Japanese ports are not allowed to be used as base for fishing boats. (2) When catching fish in the high seas, they are not allowed to be transported into various commercial ports in territorial waters for sale. (3) If fish are transported into ports or commercial ports in territorial waters for sale, they must be transported by merchant ships, and fishing boats are not allowed to enter. (4) For merchant ships carrying fish into ports, the bill of lading must be verified to prove the place of export, otherwise they will be detained. It has now consulted the two ministries of finance and foreign affairs to reschedule a meeting to avoid prolonged delays. (Special dispatch of the 14th)

(Jinan) Tang Xiang, the director of the Shandong Provincial Government Office in Beijing, arrived in Jin

Page 12

The countryside is covered in disaster victims. The Huangnitang dike collapsed on the evening of the third day, causing hundreds of houses to collapse nearby. Furthermore, yesterday, groups from the Sanshui disaster area wired for relief, claiming that the dikes in various villages and areas under Sanshui's jurisdiction, including Daliang, Yancong, Dalang, Shiban, Gaofeng, Baimu, Rongse, Tiedun, Changzhou, Yongning, Duntou, Zaogang, Mian, Shangxia Mei, Cang, Qingtang, Ruifeng, Chagang, Baishi Bao, and Pingdeng Wei, had successively collapsed. Fields and gardens were completely submerged. Tens of thousands of disaster victims are living in the open on hills, a scene of misery unseen in decades. The West River's current is swift, causing rapid torrents to surge directly towards Foshan. Consequently, the dikes near the Guangsan Railway, such as Shaobian, Xiebian, Luoge, Zhewei, Yongan, and Shangyuan, are all on the verge of collapse. Floodwater has submerged the dike tops and entered, resulting in over sixty submerged areas in Foshan's inner streets and one hundred and three submerged areas outside the city. Floodwater reached Shaobian Station by the afternoon of the fourth. On the morning of the fifth, Guangsan passenger trains suddenly announced a suspension of service because the water at Chatou Station was over a foot deep and had damaged several sleepers. After the railway bureau dispatched workers for urgent repairs, passenger and freight trains resumed normal operations in the afternoon. As for the various counties in the Dong River area, those flooded by the eastern floods from Heyuan City to the Guanyinge area have turned into a swamp, a vast expanse of water with no green grass. Inside and outside Huiyang City, places like Guankou, Tangxia, Jiangpu, Toutou, and Shaibu Changxiushui Lake are about three feet deep, and residents are using boats as transportation. The water north of Boluo City's north gate is four feet deep, and the water outside the southwest gate is over three feet deep. Additionally, it's said that the water level in the upper reaches of the Han River continues to rise, resulting in countless people and livestock drowning. (July 7th)

A Quick Letter from Wuhu: Wuhu has experienced more than ten days of heavy rain, with mountain floods and river tides surging continuously. Drainage ditches between streets and markets are overflowing, obstructing transportation. Rural embankments and dikes have been under constant repair. Last night, Baofeng Dike in the southern countryside failed despite rescue efforts, resulting in over ten thousand acres of fertile land being submerged. Several other smaller dikes have also been damaged. The provincial government, recognizing the urgent situation of the dikes during this major flood, has telegraphed the county government, urging them to step up day and night preventative measures to avoid a major disaster.

The Wuhu National Goods Company, established by former members of the Chamber of Commerce, has been in operation for two years and has made significant contributions to promoting national goods. Today, it held its founding meeting at the County Chamber of Commerce, attended by over a hundred members and representatives from various sectors. The meeting elected Wu Xingzhou, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and thirteen others, including Cui Lianggong, as directors, and Hong Wenbin as manager.

The notorious bandit Li Lao Jiu constantly gathered followers in the Wuhu countryside to commit robbery and kidnapping. After being captured by the county government and approved by the provincial government, he was taken to Yongzhen Village, the scene of his crimes, yesterday and executed by shooting.

The County Education Bureau previously planned to develop social education in Wuhu, such as opening community schools, and requested a subsidy of 5,000 yuan from the provincial government. Yesterday, they received a reply stating that social education funding should be raised locally, and there was no precedent for provincial government subsidies, making it difficult to approve the request. (13th)

Local Correspondence Suzhou Lishu Yangjiabang Robbery: Wu Er's house in Yangjiabang, Lishu Township, was suddenly approached by a bandit boat on the night of the 13th. Seven or eight bandits speaking with a Henan accent robbed seventeen shi of white rice and over forty pieces of clothing before fleeing towards Taihu Lake.

The Appeal of the Changshu Land Seizure Case Concludes: Qian Linlin and Wang Baosheng, residents of Dashiqiao Township in Changshu, colluded with the fugitive Wang Gengsong and others on March 2nd of this year to rob two privately transported opium boats, seizing twenty-seven packages of opium weighing a total of 5,721.5 taels. They transported it to Cui Jia Xiaoqiao Yao Nan Guan's house and buried it in the pigpen ash pile. After being discovered by the Zhenjiu team, Qian and others were arrested, and the original stolen goods were recovered. After a thorough investigation by the county, Qian Linlin and Wang Baosheng were each sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment, and Yao Nan Guan was sentenced to six months. Qian and others appealed to the High Court. Yesterday (14th), Judge Chen opened a court session for trial and announced the end of the debate, scheduling the sentencing for the 18th.

Wuxi Business Tax Bureau Urges Payment of First Quarter Taxes: Yang Wu Bian, the head of the local business tax collection bureau, recently determined the taxes for various businesses and sent letters to the respective trade associations, setting a deadline of the 26th for the advance payment of the first quarter's taxes. Subsequently, due to the meager amount collected, further letters were sent urging payment by the deadline. Now, more than half a month has passed, and the payment rate for various businesses remains low. This not only interferes with the province's financial needs but also hinders tax collection efforts. Yesterday, a special letter was sent to the County Chamber of Commerce requesting an investigation and prompt urging for payment by the deadline to complete the recognition of the case and facilitate collection.

Reasons for the Resignation of the Director of the Finance Bureau: Shen Ruji, the local director of the finance bureau, has repeatedly resigned to the finance department after only two months in office. Director Xu of the finance department has accepted the resignation, but Shen's intention to resign is firm. There are three reasons for this: (1) After the famine year, silver shipment income has drastically decreased, and there is no financial solution other than borrowing to maintain operations. (2) The First Section Chief and the Chief of Disbursement have resolutely resigned, causing great mental distress. (3) Due to a pre-existing stomach ailment, the workload is overwhelming, hence the resolute resignation.

A Sailing Boat on the Changzhou Xiaohe River is Robbed En Route: A sailing boat departing from Xiaohe Town, Changzhou, for the city on the evening of the 12th was traveling from Xiaohe Town to the city when, around 4:00 AM on the morning of the 13th, five or six bandits suddenly fired shots and ordered the boat to stop. The bandits boarded the boat and robbed over thirty passengers, causing losses of over 300 yuan. The boat owner suffered losses of over 100 yuan. An old man selling Shaya medicine was shot in the hand. After the incident, nearby police stations pursued the bandits, but they had already fled far away.

The County Magistrate Zhang's Beloved Nephew Drowns: Zhang Pengzhu, the magistrate of Wuyi County, had a nephew named Xiyao whom he loved dearly. Currently a student at National Jiaotong University, he recently accompanied his younger sister Taoyun to take the entrance examination for the Provincial Women's Normal School. The day before yesterday, he was escorting his sister back to Yixing by boat. At the Yixing dock, Zhang was standing at the bow of the boat when it suddenly turned sharply and collided with a bridge foundation, causing him to lose his footing and fall into the water. Despite immediate rescue attempts, it was too late.

Dike Collapse Causes Disaster: The dike built at San Wei Port in the Fourth District of Wuyi to block the flow of the Yangtze River collapsed yesterday morning amid continuous rain and a sudden surge in the river level. In an instant, the river water breached the dike, turning nearby fields into a swamp. Within moments, the water reached depths of three to four zhang, and residents were forced to flee with their belongings.

A Passenger Carrying Guns and Ammunition is Apprehended in Zhenjiang: Officer Wang of the Jiangbian Fifth Precinct's First Branch was patrolling the river mouth yesterday when a small river boat arrived in Zhenjiang. Noticing a person behaving nervously, he searched them and discovered ten bullets. The person claimed to be a former member of the Taixing Security Regiment who was mistakenly carrying the ammunition. However, due to the suspicious nature of the matter, Officer Wang deemed it related to military supplies and presented it to the Fifth Precinct, which in turn transferred it to headquarters for further action.

Nantong Investigates Local 2 Million Yuan Public Debt: The Nantong Financial Restructuring Committee has decided to investigate the 2 million yuan local public debt issued by Zhang Xiaoruo when he was in charge of the Autonomous Association. They will first send a letter to Zhang Xiaoruo, requesting a response within ten days regarding the handling process, before determining the next steps.

Water Disaster Disputes in Dongxiang Intensify: The severe flooding in Dongxiang, Nantong, has submerged fields and houses, leading to a tragic disaster. Disputes between upstream and downstream areas over water discharge and dike breaches remain unresolved. Continuous heavy rain has further raised the water level. Three districts in the downstream area believe the floodgates should be closed due to rising tides, while the upstream area continues to discharge water without consultation, leading to over a thousand villagers confronting those in the downstream areas. The county government has strongly discouraged this and telegraphed representatives from each district, calling an emergency meeting to discuss a fair resolution.

Gaoyou Suffers Disaster from Torrential Rain, Flooding Embankment Fields: The county had received a foot of rain in the preceding days without significant impact on the crops. However, yesterday (11th), a sudden downpour began around 2:00 PM and continued until 4:00 AM this morning. Rivers and harbors in the rural areas overflowed their banks, completely submerging low-lying fields. Even the high-lying embankment fields in the vicinity of the city, including the Fifth General Headquarters, the Seventh and Fifth General Headquarters, Shuangmiao, and the First Zone, collapsed successively during the night, creating a vast expanse of water. The water level in the Qianjiahuo and Yanglao Dike areas of the southern countryside is also high, and efforts are underway to bail out the water.

A Bather Scalded to Death, Bathhouse Owner Arrested: The owner of the Nanyuan Bathhouse in Qianguan Lane was arrested after an unidentified bather was scalded to death after falling asleep in the pool and tumbling into the hot water vat. The bathhouse owner moved the body to an empty house and ordered the town warden to bury it but it came to the attention of the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday (10th) evening, the police were instructed to arrest the bathhouse owner, Zhai Er, and transfer him to the county government for trial. After a brief investigation, bail was set pending an official inquest.

Luzhou Kidnappers and Hostages Escorted to Luzhou: Wang, the wife of a resident surnamed Zhang in Siqian, a village in the southern part of Luzhou County, took her young son to her mother's home in Shenjiawan in March of this year. On the way, they were kidnapped. Both the Zhang and Wang families reported the incident to the county and sent people to investigate, but without success. On the 22nd of last month, the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team rescued Zhang Wang and her son from danger at the Shunhe Hotel on Beiler Road in the French Concession and arrested five kidnappers, including Li Zhengming. The Municipal Public Security Bureau sent a letter to the Wuxing Public Security Bureau's Detective Team to inform Wang's family. After receiving the news, the family applied to the county government and then to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to escort them back. It is reported that Wang and her son, as well as the five kidnappers, including Li Zhengming, were escorted to Luzhou the day before yesterday.

Hangzhou Appeals for Exemption from Salt Boat Conscription: The Zhejiang Transportation Office sent a letter to the Provincial Government yesterday, citing a report from the Zhejiang East Changguang Open Line Merchant Executive Committee, stating that Zhejiang East's line salt relies entirely on boats for transportation. According to recent reports, the army is conscripting salt boats in Zhejiang to suppress bandits in Jiangxi, resulting in salt being abandoned along the coast. An appeal has been made for assistance. Therefore, the letter requests the office to consult with the Provincial Government and instruct all military and police agencies to exempt salt boats from conscription in order to ensure the people's food supply.

Comparative Increase in Various Tax Revenues: The Hangzhou Municipal Government Finance Bureau completed the compilation of various tax revenues for the second half of the 19th year under the direction of former Director Ye. The total actual revenue was 489,560 yuan, exceeding the budgeted amount by over 42,200 yuan, and an increase of over 40,680 yuan compared to the 18th year.

Flood Disasters in Various Counties of Zhejiang Province: Due to continuous heavy rain in various counties of Zhejiang Province, flood disasters have been reported. Counties such as Hangzhou, Ninghai, Chun'an, and Suian have telegraphed the Zhejiang Relief Association for assistance. It is now learned that the Wukang County Government also sent a telegram to the province yesterday, reporting that the northeastern villages of the county, which are low-lying, have suffered flood disasters due to continuous heavy rain and rising water levels, resulting in the complete submersion of spring flowers and seedlings. Furthermore, the silkworm harvest only achieved two-tenths of the previous year's yield, leaving the people destitute. An urgent appeal has been made for relief efforts to save lives.

Ningbo Zhenhai County Magistrate Regains Freedom: Zhenhai County Magistrate Cao Boquan, after being impeached by the Supervisory Yuan, had Zheng Yu sent to Zhenhai by the Provincial Civil Affairs Department to serve as acting county magistrate, and Cao Boquan was detained. It is now learned that Acting County Magistrate Zheng Yu presented to the Provincial Government the question of whether Cao Boquan should continue to be detained now that Cao Boquan has clearly handed over affairs. Yesterday, an order was received from the Provincial Government that he should be released from continued detention. However, it is not yet known whether Cao will be reinstated.

Bandits Kidnap and Burn Houses: The homes of Yuan Zuopei and Yuan Afu, residents of Yuanjiaao in Fenghua, were quite wealthy. Yesterday at midnight, over twenty bandits suddenly arrived. Zuopei was out, and they could not find him. They then went to Afu's house, kidnapped Afu, and burned down Yuan Zuopei's house, which spread to neighboring houses, destroying a total of eighteen houses, with losses exceeding ten thousand gold. The villagers were in a state of panic.

Xiao Shan Murderer Sentenced to Twelve Years: Chu Xiaomao, also known as Maomao, of Gaojiali in Xixiang, Xiao Shan, was found guilty of murdering his friend Tang Jinlin last winter. The case was transferred by the Wenyan Public Security Branch to the court, which repeatedly investigated the matter and detained him in prison. The defendant was sentenced on the 12th by Criminal Court Judge Fu Tingrui. As a result, Chu Xiaomao was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment for the crime of preparing to commit murder, and deprived of public rights for fourteen years.

Mountain Fields Suffer Another Major Flood Disaster: From around 9:00 PM on the 12th until the morning of the 13th, there was torrential rain, resulting in extensive damage to mountain fields. Much of the early rice, which was already heading, was submerged, resulting in particularly heavy losses. Additionally, two Jiaolong waterspouts emerged in Zhengjiali, Jinyi Mountain, with water reaching five feet high on level ground. Another Jiaolong waterspout emerged in Zhangyi, Qingshan, destroying over ten acres of fields. Today (13th), the fields along the river are either submerged or damaged, resulting in significant losses for the farmers, who are visibly worried.

Educational News Highlights Hunan Province's Vocational School Reorganization Measures: The Ministry of Education received from the Hunan Provincial Department of Education five measures for reorganizing vocational schools in Hunan Province and requested instructions. The Ministry of Education instructed: "The submitted documents have been noted. The proposed measures for reorganizing vocational schools are temporarily approved for record-keeping until the Ministry's Vocational School Organization Law is promulgated. The request to extend the deadline for the registration of private vocational schools to September 1st is approved. Please be informed accordingly."

Attachment: Hunan Province's Vocational School Reorganization Measures: (1) Standardize the names of vocational schools at all levels: (A) Agricultural, industrial, and commercial schools that enroll junior high school graduates or those with equivalent qualifications may apply to the Ministry of Education to be called Senior Vocational Schools in a specific subject and may continue to be called middle schools. (B) Vocational schools that enroll higher elementary school graduates or those with equivalent qualifications may be called Vocational Schools. (C) Vocational schools that enroll primary school graduates or those with equivalent qualifications shall be called Simple Vocational Schools. (2) Stipulate the minimum amount of operating expenses for vocational schools at all levels. The operating expenses for vocational schools in category A of the preceding article shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 26 of the Regulations for Private Schools. The start-up costs for vocational schools in category B shall be at least 10,000 yuan, and the operating expenses shall be at least 8,000 yuan. The start-up costs for vocational schools in category C shall be at least 8,000 yuan, and the operating expenses shall be at least 3,000 yuan. Existing vocational schools at all levels whose start-up costs and operating expenses do not meet the aforementioned minimum requirements shall be funded by the responsible party. Vocational schools at all levels newly established whose start-up costs and operating expenses do not meet the aforementioned minimum requirements shall not be registered. (3) Matters related to the registration and reporting of vocational schools: (A) All existing private vocational schools shall follow the Regulations for Private Schools and the orders of the Ministry of Education and submit various forms to the Department of Education for registration by September 1st of this year. Schools in category B or higher shall also report to the Ministry for record-keeping. (B) When submitting the enrollment forms for new students and transfer students, vocational schools at all levels shall submit the original graduation certificates or transfer certificates from the previous school to the Department of Education. (4) Enrich the content of vocational schools: (A) Vocational schools at all levels shall establish factories and emphasize student labor. (B) Unless otherwise stipulated by laws and regulations, the time students at all levels of vocational schools spend on production and work shall not be less than the time spent on written instruction. (C) Students at all levels of vocational schools shall not be allowed to graduate without the ability to engage in production. (5) These measures shall be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation.

The Jiangsu Social Education Summer Workshop Opens: In order to utilize the summer vacation to study social education theory and practical problems, promote the progress of implementation methods, and facilitate smooth implementation, Jiangsu Provincial Social Education Institutions, such as the Institute of Education and the People's Education Center, are holding a Social Education Summer Workshop from the 10th of this month to the 9th of August at the Wuxi Provincial Institute of Education. Gao Jian Si, the president of the institute, is in charge of all matters, and Lei Bin Nan is the director of academic affairs. Staff currently serving or having served in social education institutions across the province are being recruited to attend the lectures, with a maximum of five people from each county. The expenses are subsidized by the Education Bureau. The lecturers and subjects include: Jiang Wen Yu, Vocational Guidance and Personnel Guidance; Zhang Yao Xiang, Adult Learning Psychology; Pan Guang Dan, Problems of Chinese Families; Lou Tong Sun, Introduction to Consumer Cooperative Movement; Liu Nan Hai, Population Problems of China; Cai Zheng Ya, Social Survey and Statistics; Tang Qi Yu, Land Problems of China; Zhao Bu Xia, Social Education Administration; Du Ding You, Implementation Methods of Libraries and Adult Education; Yu Song Hua, Social Problems; Wang Zhi Xin, Rural Economy, Introduction to Rural Cooperative Movement; Zhao Guang Tao, Organization and Implementation of People's Education Centers; Sun Zhong Wei, Outline of Agricultural Extension, Organization and Implementation of Farmers' Education Centers; Qin Feng Xiang, Zhuyin Symbols; Zhu Ji Qing, Public Health and First Aid; Ma Zu Wu, Implementation Methods of Urban People's Schools; Gao Jian Si, Introduction to Social Education, Livelihood Education for the People; Lei Bin Nan, Comparative Adult Education; Gan Dao Bo, Political Education for the People, Implementation Methods of Rural People's Schools; Li Ji Xin, Problems of Rural Subsidiary Industries; Qiu You Zhen, The Three Principles of the People and the Principles of Social Evolution; Xu Gong Jian, Inspection and Guidance of People's Education; Fang Tian You, Editing of People's Reading Materials; Xu Xu, People's Library Education; Wang Geng Tao, People's Health Education; Lu Li Cheng, Guidance on Cattle Raising; Chen Shou Tong, Cooperative Organizations; Tang Song Jia Wei, Selection of Seeds and Promotion of Seed Selection Methods; Yu Shou Mei, Organization and Implementation of People's Tea Gardens; Chen Rui Zhang, Guidance on People's Entertainment, etc. It is reported that the conference started its classes yesterday, with over a hundred students actually attending.

Opening of the Zhejiang Summer Workshop: Shao Peizi Reports, Shen Fuzhai Delivers a Speech, Fang Dingzhong and Xie Xunchu Speak. The summer in-service training workshop for educational service personnel, jointly established by National Zhejiang University and the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, held its opening ceremony in the auditorium of Zhejiang University at 7:30 AM yesterday. Over four to five hundred lecturers, students, and guests attended. After the ceremony, Shao Peizi, the president of Zhejiang University, reported on the preparation process and future plans for the summer workshop. Next, Shen Fuzhai delivered a speech on behalf of the Director of the Department of Education, briefly stating that educational service personnel in various regions have always focused on academic advancement but have neglected the improvement of teaching methods. Therefore, the purpose of this workshop is to enable educational service personnel in various regions to supplement their knowledge and improve their methods. Fang Dingzhong then spoke on the importance of popular education and how to make education practical and not superficial. Finally, lecturer Xie Xunchu spoke on how to make education a specialized profession. After the speeches, Zheng Xiaocang reported on the changes in the curriculum, and the bell rang for class. It is reported that the first day of courses included Chen Kemei's Principles of Education and Modern Education Trends for the middle school group, Zhang Yisan's Middle School Teaching Methods, Chen Kemei's Principles of Education for the elementary education group, and Zhao Buxia's Introduction to People's Education for the social education group.

June Education Fees for Wuxian City Schools to be Distributed: The Wuxian Education Bureau announced that the 19th year for various schools and social education institutions has ended, but the June education fees have not yet been collected and distributed. In order to show consideration for the poor teachers and clarify procedures, they have worked hard to raise funds and have reached an agreement. The Local Japanese Research Association Moves from Shanghai to Nanjing: Inviting Dai Jitao as Chairman. The Japanese Research Association, organized by students who studied in Japan, sent representatives Liu Baimin, Ma Zongrong, Liu Jialun, Zhou Xianwen, and Xu Diaoxi to Shanghai. Last night, they hosted the Shanghai press at Gongdelin on Pike Road, with over twenty people attending. Liu Baimin chaired the meeting. After some drinking, Mr. Liu stood up and reported that the association was established in the autumn of the 18th year of the Republic of China, with its headquarters in Tokyo. It currently has over two thousand members and publishes a monthly magazine called "Japan." For the sake of facilitating the association's activities, the headquarters was moved to Nanjing in May, with branch offices established at various important locations at home and abroad to facilitate communication. President Dai Jitao has been invited to be the chairman of the association. Future plans include continuing to publish the Japan magazine, collecting materials, publishing Japanese research books, convening lectures on Japanese issues whenever possible, and establishing a library for research on Manchuria and Mongolia. Since the incident of the massacre of overseas Chinese by Koreans, the association's members have been extremely indignant, sending letters and telegrams back and forth. They have also sent personnel to Incheon to investigate the truth on the ground and have collected important materials on the massacre at a high price, compiling a special issue on the Korean case for distribution to the people of the country to serve as a warning. Ma Zongrong then spoke about the Japanese's conspiracy regarding the Wanbao Mountain incident. The press was addressed by Xu Tinglang. The meeting adjourned around 9:00 PM.

Opening Ceremony of the Third District Summer Workshop: The Jiangsu Province Third District Elementary School Teachers' Summer Workshop reported the day before yesterday. A total of 221 people attended from Shanghai (24), Nanhui (24), Qingpu (24), Fengxian (28), Chuansha (8), Songjiang (23), Jinshan (26), Jiading (20), Chongming (21), and Baoshan (23). The opening ceremony was held at the junior high school department of Shanghai Middle School at 9:00 AM yesterday. Director Zheng Xigu, Chairman Hou Baosan, and Committee Member Shi Yangyong attended, as well as guests including Director Zheng of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, staff members, lecturers, and over three hundred students. After the ceremony, the director delivered a speech, stating that modern educational service personnel have three major weaknesses: physical fitness, diligence, and academic advancement are all inversely proportional to their years of service. If we want to take responsibility for reforming Chinese education, we must start with ourselves and deeply consider and improve the above three weaknesses in order to have any hope. The chairman, committee member, Director Zheng, and representative of the county education bureau, Shi Yangyong, then delivered speeches. Photography concluded the ceremony around 12:00 PM. The staff and lecturers of the conference are listed below: Director Zheng Xigu, Chairman Committee Member Hou Baosan, Committee Members: the heads of the education bureaus of the ten counties of Shanghai, Chuansha, Nanhui, Jinshan, Baoshan, Jiading, Chongming, Fengxian, Songjiang, and Qingpu, Academic Affairs: Zhang Zhonghuan and Chen Yue, Dormitory Affairs: Tian Dianan, General Affairs: Zhao Weizu, Party Doctrine Lecturer: Pan Gongzhan, Zhuyin Symbol Lecturer: Ma Guoying, Elementary School Administration Lecturer: Sheng Langxi, Elementary School Discipline Problems Lecturer: Zheng Xigu, Rural Education Lecturer: Jiang Wenyu, Education Statistics Lecturer: Shen Yougan, Education Measurement Lecturer: Chen Xuan Shan, Single-Grade Teaching Method Lecturer: Chen Xianke, Elementary School Equipment Lecturers: Wang Weizhi and Yu Aichen. Special lectures include: Huang Renzhi, "Elementary School Teachers and the World Situation," Huang Jingsi, "Rural Education," Shen Yizhen, "Educational Trends," He Yangxian, "Cooperation Theory," Liao Maoru, "Measurement Problems," Xie Xunchu, "Learning Psychology," and Wang Yunwu, "Scientific Management Methods." There will also be extracurricular activity discussions and single-grade education discussions, with knowledgeable and experienced people participating in the discussions. There will be an exam after each subject is taught. The timetable has been arranged, and classes will begin on time yesterday. An entertainment party is scheduled for the evening of July 31, and a closing ceremony will be held on the morning of August 1.

Sports Hong Kong China-Portugal South Tour Competition Schedule Finalized: Thirteen matches from August 1st to August 30th. A performance in Hong Kong against the Hong Kong Army on the 12th. A Man Collapses in a Pool of Blood

Outside the South Railway Station in Yangqi West Fence Lane on the Tracks

At approximately 7:00 AM yesterday, railway workers discovered a man lying in a pool of blood by the side of the tracks outside the Shanghai South Railway Station in Yangqi West Fence Lane. The man appeared to be in his twenties, dressed in a short blue striped cloth shirt, with a white undershirt underneath. He wore gray cloth trousers and had a flat-topped hairstyle. He had two gold teeth inlaid in his mouth and was barefoot. Barely clinging to life, it was evident that he had been assassinated, with several knife wounds, including injuries to the side of his head and left ear. The incident was reported to the Gaochang Temple Second District Police Station, and Inspector Gao dispatched officers to investigate. The injured man was transported to the Xinpu Yutang hospital for treatment. Due to the severity of his injuries, it is feared he may not survive. Nearby residents reported hearing someone crying out urgently around 4:00 AM that night. However, due to the remote and desolate nature of the area, they were afraid to investigate.

A Man and Woman Attempt Suicide by Poison - One Dies, One Survives

Dong Zixiang Driven to Suicide by Poverty

Ma Alan Fortunate to be Rescued

On the night of the 11th of this month, in Room 11 of the Beizhan Hotel, located at No. 5 Jielu Road in the North Railway Station area, a guest named Dong Chenxue from Wuxi (alias Ma Shouxiang), aged 26, attempted suicide by poisoning due to economic hardship. Dong succumbed to the poison and died. Ms. Ma was barely alive and was transported to Guangren Hospital for treatment. Ms. Ma's condition improved due to the lighter dose of poison and the timely medical intervention, and she was revived by the next day. Yesterday morning, detectives from the Huishi Police Station brought Ma Alan from Guangren Hospital and escorted her to the Second Criminal Court of the Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, presented the case, stating that around 1:00 PM yesterday, the Beizhan Hotel at No. 309 North Shanxi Road reported to the Chinese constables that a man and a woman in Room 11 had attempted suicide by poison. The constables reported this to the police station, who dispatched detectives to investigate. They found the man dead and the woman barely alive. The woman was taken to Guangren Hospital. An autopsy revealed that they had ingested opium. The man's body was taken to the Féi Lun Road morgue. By 10:00 PM that night, the woman regained consciousness and identified herself as Ma Alan, 22 years old, from Wuxi. She stated that the deceased was named Ma Shouxiang, though he used the name Dong Chenxue at the hotel. She claimed they had decided to commit suicide together due to their inability to find work and extreme poverty, purchasing opium to share. They consumed the opium at midnight on the 11th, each taking a box. She ate hers first and then lost consciousness. She woke up to find Ma Shouxiang dead. She insisted that their suicide attempt was voluntary and that there was no coercion involved. Judge Ge Zhitan questioned if she was hiding some unspoken pain. Ma Alan replied that she was alone and destitute, suffering from economic hardship, and had decided to end her life after much deliberation, stating that there was nothing else to add, crying as she spoke. Judge Ge then adjourned the case until the 21st of this month and ordered the police to take Ms. Ma away. She was immediately sent to the morgue. Meanwhile, Prosecutor Guo Wei from the Special District Court arrived at the morgue to examine Ma Shouxiang's body. During his examination, a witness named Zhu Huanzhen testified that he was a friend of the deceased, whose real name was Dong Zixiang, from Wuxi. He said Dong had an elderly mother, a wife, and a three-year-old daughter at home. Zhu had not seen Dong recently and was unaware of the circumstances of his suicide. He came to claim the body after seeing the news report. After Ma Alan gave her testimony, Prosecutor Guo stated that the autopsy revealed that Dong Zixiang had died from opium poisoning. Since the police had filed charges against Ma Alan, also known as Ma Mashi, she should be handed over to the court. The body was released to Zhu Huangen, a friend, for funeral arrangements after he signed a guarantee.

A Laborer Dies After Jumping from a Vehicle

Yesterday at 5:00 PM, near the Tilanqiao Pei Kai'er Road, a sanitation truck of the Public Works Department, numbered 16693, was traveling along the road when a laborer jumped off the vehicle. The rear wheels crushed his skull, and he died instantly. After the incident, a patrol officer arrived and transported the body to the morgue for examination.

Lu Youcai Struck and Killed by a Car - Investigation

Around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, a Chinese constable numbered 2304 from the Huishi Police Station was patrolling Jingzhou Road when he saw four or five children playing with slingshots made of leather straps and wire. As he approached to disperse them, a 15-year-old boy named Lu Youcai ran north on Pei Kai'er Road and crossed the street when a truck numbered 9335 sped by, hitting and killing him. The officer transported the body to the Féi Lun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the Special District Court assigned Prosecutor Guo to examine the body. During his examination, the boy's father, Lu Baozhu, stated that he would file a lawsuit with the Special District Court for his son's tragic death. Prosecutor Guo stated that the autopsy confirmed that Lu Youcai had been killed by vehicle number 9335 and ordered the body be released to his father for funeral arrangements.

Xu Renquan Seeks Justice for His Sister

Xu Renquan of Gaoyou submitted a petition to the District Court yesterday, stating that his sister, Wang Xu Mashi, 31, was married to Wang Tingchen from Yangzhou, who resided at No. 1 Jiade Lane, Xietu Road. She was subjected to abuse. On the 11th of this month, Wang severely beat his wife, and she fled to her sister's home. After being persuaded to return, word came that she had died suddenly. Having arrived in Shanghai from Changzhou three days later, he examined his sister's body and found two bruises on her waist and ribs, indicating that she had died from her injuries. When her sister inquired, Wang claimed she had died of a sudden illness. He believes the conflicting information is highly suspicious. He requests an investigation to seek justice. Chief Prosecutor Liu ordered the body to be brought to the court for examination.

Public Bus Accident Case

The Chinese Ratepayers Association Requests the Public Works Department to Investigate

Yesterday, the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the Public Works Department regarding the case of Public Bus No. 15015 hitting a pedestrian on Di Siwei Road. It stated, "According to a letter from Huang Mao Mashi, her son, Lin Nian, was riding a bicycle on Di Siwei Road around 10:00 AM on July 4th when Public Bus No. 15015, speeding from behind, struck the bicycle, knocking him down and fracturing his leg. He lost consciousness and was taken to Tongren Hospital by the police. He is currently in critical condition. The police have not yet initiated an investigation. We respectfully request that you instruct the Public Works Department to investigate the matter according to the law and order the responsible party to provide medical expenses and support for the family." Vehicle accidents must be investigated according to the law. We hope that you will investigate and handle the matter accordingly.

Striving Against the Repeated Levying of Business Tax on Manufactured Goods

The Scientific Instrument Hall Sends Another Letter to the Chamber of Commerce

The Scientific Instrument Hall sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce stating: "(The above is omitted) What our hall wants to know is whether the same capital owner should be levied twice for the business tax if the manufacturing location is separate from the sales location. What we want your association to strive for is that the same manufactured goods under the same capital owner should not be repeatedly levied due to the separation of manufacturing and sales locations. This is not that the ministry's orders are unclear. Now the Ministry of Finance has not explained the principle of levy to the whole country, but only added an explanation to the previous order, fearing that it is not enough to make people satisfied. We believe that your association is deeply versed in law and economics. We hope that you will thoroughly explore according to economic principles, or visit economic experts, or legal accounting teachers, to seek their correction. If the ministry's orders are appropriate, it should be announced to all industries and be followed. If the ministry's orders are inappropriate, it should present a request for relief to the Legislative Yuan based on academic principles, so that good taxes will not turn into harmful business. This is what we sincerely pray for. In modern times, industry is prosperous and cities are flourishing. Manufacturing is mostly in the industrial zone, and sales are in the commercial zone. The two locations cannot be separated. The manufactured goods from the manufacturing location are wholesaled to the sales location, and there is no sale behavior. The manufactured goods delivered from the manufacturing location to the sales location only notify the cost and do not add any profit. When the sales location wholesale, it is based on the cost, considering the market situation, and determining the price. For example, handling documents, the manufacturer drafts it, and the seller verifies and issues it. How can it be said that these are two things? Moreover, direct wholesale in the factory and setting up a sales office away from the manufacturing location have different procedures, but the nature is the same. It is like judicial supervision and other institutions. Because the institution's affairs are not complicated, each department is in the same institution. If the Executive Yuan is separated from each department, it cannot be said that the relationship between the Executive Yuan and the other four institutions is different. Our hall准情度理, in fact, is still confused about the re-levying of business tax on manufactured goods. Please give detailed instructions and check the handling, I am very fortunate.

Wu Jingtai Pays Attention to Foreign Merchants' Deeds

Mr. Wu Jingxiong, advisor to the Public Works Department of the Public Concession, told a Guowen News Agency reporter yesterday that his report to the Public Works Department is in progress and may need to follow the example of advisor Fei Tang to solicit opinions on various municipal administration matters from various groups in this city for reference. However, Mr. Wu paid particular attention to the issue of deeds because many Chinese merchants' real estate and land are registered under foreign merchants' names. This is enough to increase the tax amount for foreigners, and Chinese merchants who pay a large amount of taxes are not actually getting the benefits. He plans to study this issue in detail and find a proper solution. However, these are all things that people are doing. As for the responsibilities borne by the Public Works Department, they are matters that the board of directors of the Public Works Department cannot solve, that is, to solicit opinions from me to find a solution.

The owner of Jiuyu Tang paper fan shop, for the eighth anniversary of the shop, has spent months collecting fine fan paintings by more than 40 famous artists in Shanghai, including Cheng Yaosheng, Shen Xinhai, Wu Daiqiu, Ma Mengrong, Xiao Wuquan, Zhao Duru, Feng Chaoran, Wang Yiting, Shang Shengbo, Huang Binhong, Zhang Shanzi, Zhang Daqian, Ma Gongyu, and Wang Ershui, totaling more than 300 pieces. All fans on display and those ordered at the exhibition will be reduced by 10% to express our appreciation. It is said that the works are all masterpieces of first-class famous artists and are extremely valuable. A collection of Ma Mengrong's colored flower, bird, grass, and insect fans is also very exquisite. Those who are interested should not miss this opportunity.

A Shot Rings Out at the End of Datong Road

Someone Cries for Help

The Bandits' Whereabouts are Unknown

Around 11:00 PM the night before last, at the north end of Datong Road in Zhabei, bandits fired a shot, and someone cried for help. Since there were no patrol officers nearby, the Pengpu Security Team's second team rushed to investigate after hearing the sound, but the bandits were gone. Upon further investigation, it was learned from nearby Jiangbei shantytown residents that a large man wearing a blue cloth short shirt and trousers and a man wearing a black gown fired a shot at a man wearing a silk gown. Fortunately, they missed, and they fled in different directions. Because it was late at night and dark, it was unknown where they fled.

Robbery Case Goes to Trial

Liu Huicheng Recovers and Appears in Court

Both Defendants Deny Robbery

Liu Huicheng, a native of Nanjing and an accountant at the Tianzhang Paper Mill at the Huangpu Wharf in Yangshupu, obtained a salary of 1,258 yuan at the mill's office on Aiduya Road on the afternoon of the 6th of this month. As he rode the No. 9 bus back to the mill, he was stopped by three robbers near the Changjiang Cinema. They stabbed Liu in the back of the head with a knife and robbed him of his money. Liu Kunjin, a passerby, captured one of the robbers, Liu Ji, a native of Qingkou, and recovered 350 yuan. The Huishi Police Station later apprehended another accomplice, Xu Abao, a native of Yong, and found two knives on him. They were sent to the Special District Court for trial. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide opened the court to continue the trial. Police lawyer Li Zhishan stated that the investigation of other accomplices was still ongoing. Now that Liu Huicheng has recovered from his injuries and is present in court, he requests his testimony. Liu Huicheng then testified about the circumstances of the robbery. He was unable to identify the robbers' faces. When questioned, Liu Ji claimed that he was just passing by and found a paper package on the ground, denying the robbery. Xu Abao claimed that Ah Fu, who was at large, was the one who robbed Liu Huicheng. He stated that he and Ah Fu were invited to wait in Changjiang Lane next to the Changjiang Cinema. Each of them carried a knife. The police detective stated that both defendants confessed at the police station that Ah Fu invited them to wait in Changjiang Lane next to the Changjiang Cinema. Each of them carried a knife, and their confessions were written down. Liu Huicheng and Chen Chongqing, the deputy manager of the mill, were present when the confessions were written down. Judge Feng then read the confessions aloud, but both defendants denied them. Liu and Chen testified that the defendants' confessions at the police station matched the written confessions. Judge Feng then ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody and adjourned the trial.

Xue Bin Repeatedly Extorted People

The Matter Was Exposed, and He Fled to Hankou

He Was Arrested Upon Returning to Shanghai

The owner of Zhou Songhe Redwood Shop at No. 134 Huiguan Street in the South City received three letters from extortionists in December of last year, demanding 1,000 yuan. The shop owner reported the matter to the police station, and following the instructions in the letter regarding the meeting place at No. 71 Haichao Temple Road outside Xiaonanmen in the South City, the police arrested Yao Baoshan. During questioning, Yao claimed that he had been deceived by Xue Bin, the owner of Xuechang Machinery Factory at No. 128 Xiaoximen. The police went to arrest Xue, but he had already fled to Hankou. It wasn't until the day before yesterday that Dong Mingde, the leader of the first district of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's detective team, learned that Xue had returned to Shanghai and was taking a bath in a bathhouse at the Wangjia Que intersection. They rushed there and arrested Xue Bin. During questioning, he claimed to be 22 years old, from Anhui. He admitted that he, Gu Shulong, Wang Benxiang, and Zhu Xingquan, who ran the Guangyuan Printing House on Daxing Street outside Xiaoximen, had extorted Zhou Songhe, the owner of the redwood shop, last year. He said he had only returned to Shanghai in March of this year and had joined Gu and others in extorting Luo Yide, the owner of the Luo Yide Leather Shop at No. 154 Jiaozhou Road in the British Concession, and Wang Dexing, a resident at No. 44 Haige Road. In April, they also extorted Yao Deben, a resident of Xiaomaoqiao in Longhua. They had divided all the stolen money and spent it. The case was handed over to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

A Mother-in-Law and Daughter-in-Law Quarrel, Leading to a Suicide Attempt

Liu Daxian's Poisoning Incident

Liu Daxian, a 58-year-old from Tongzhou, lived at No. 8 Huade Lane, Huade Road. He was fond of drinking. Yesterday afternoon, he blamed his daughter-in-law for cooking the dishes too salty. His daughter-in-law did not respond. He continued to scold her, and she retorted. Liu became angry and decided to end his life. He took advantage of a moment when no one was watching and swallowed raw opium. Soon after, he was poisoned and barely alive. His family found him and rushed him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. According to the doctor, Liu had taken too much poison and was in danger of dying.

Architect Wu Jingqi Returns to China

Mr. Wu Jingqi, a native of Guangdong, is 30 years old. He graduated from Lingnan University with a Bachelor of Arts degree and then went to the United States to study architecture at the University of Pennsylvania, obtaining Bachelor and Master of Architecture degrees. He was a professor of arts and crafts at Lingnan Middle School and a teaching assistant in watercolor painting at the University of Pennsylvania and interned at architectural firms in New York and Pennsylvania. He arrived in Shanghai on the 8th of this month and joined Fan Wenzhao Architect Firm at No. 29 Sichuan Road as an assistant architect.

Yu Jichuan Leaves for Hunan to Take Up a Position in the Provincial Committee

The newly appointed Hunan Provincial Committee member Yu Jichuan, urged by frequent telegrams from Hunan He, left Shanghai yesterday with former Hunan Construction Department Director Song Hegeng to take up his post in Hunan. Mr. Yu is a Bachelor of Science in Civil Engineering from the University of Illinois in the United States. He has served as an engineer for various highways in Hunan and the United States Associated Press Radio Station, as well as the head professor of the Civil Engineering Department of Fudan and Donghua Universities, the section chief of the Hubei Construction Department, the director of the Wuhan Municipal Public Works Bureau, and the director of the Changsha Municipal Government. He has recently served as a senior technician of the Central Construction Committee and the deputy director of the National Irrigation Bureau. He is enthusiastic about construction and has achieved remarkable results in Hunan and Hubei provinces. It is believed that he will contribute many suggestions to the Hunan government this time.

Publication of Automobile Driving Law

The Automobile Driving Law, written by Ding Zuzhe and published by the Commercial Press, has now been published, priced at 60 cents per copy. In addition to explaining the driving methods of various automobiles in detail, this book also describes the automobile protection methods and is a must-read for those who study driving and use automobiles. The book contains 49 illustrations, making it easy to understand. The entire book is divided into 15 chapters, the content of the first chapter is an introduction, the second chapter is an explanation of automobile machinery, the third chapter is an explanation of automobile driving organs, the fourth chapter is what you should know before driving, the fifth chapter is the preparation before driving, the sixth chapter is the opening method of ordinary automobiles, the seventh chapter is the usage of Ford automobiles, the eighth chapter is the opening method of new cars, the ninth chapter is what you should know before buying a new car, the tenth chapter is what you should know before buying an old car, the eleventh chapter is the automobile protection law, the twelfth chapter is the water tank protection law, the thirteenth chapter is the tire protection law, the fourteenth chapter is the inspection and repair of engine problems, and the fifteenth chapter is the occurrence, treatment, and prevention of automobile fires.

Free Talk - A Thought

Autumn Water

Hatred is the only weapon of the weak against the strong.

"Disobedience" is one of the virtues because it is difficult to distinguish from "Don't care." "Don't care" is the most common and most inert evil in the world.

Not being loved does not hinder the progress of one's career. However, not being respected will lead to nothing.

If there is deceit between friends, they are not good friends.

As long as you can make money, you are a social celebrity and a national leader.

If the heart of a great man is completely revealed to people, he will be stabbed to death immediately by others.

The love of modern men and women is like chewing gum. At the beginning, the taste is mellow and interesting. After chewing for a long time, it feels bland and tasteless. It must be spit out and replaced with another one.

Students do not know the pain of unemployment until after graduation. Therefore, to fundamentally alleviate unemployment, it is best to close all schools in the world.

Those who do charity work are quite similar to the lustful Dengtuzi. On the surface, they hate the growth of evil deeds, but in reality, they are cultivating evil deeds themselves.

No matter how big or small, its success must have corresponding conditions. Therefore, there is absolutely no absolute freedom in the world.

Record of Yitong River

Wang Wu

The Wanbaoshan Incident is now raging. The brutality of the Koreans is increasing day by day, involving overseas Chinese in Korea. The Chinese in Pyongyang and Incheon were attacked by Korean brutality, with thousands of deaths and injuries, and losses exceeding hundreds of millions. It is truly an unexpected misfortune. The details of all the events have been recorded in various newspapers. What is described now is just a passage from a travelogue of Yitong River.

In July of the 29th year of Guangxu, I was ordered by the Ministry of Posts and Communications to go to Manchuria and Mongolia to install telegraph poles. A total of 800,000 telegraph poles were used, all transported by the Yitong River and distributed along the river. The Yitong River has two branches. One is the Yitong Line, which is 998 li long and can be used for boating and carrying goods. In summer and autumn, when the water rises, steamships can pass. The other is the Gongzhuling Line, which is 352 li long. When the water rises, rafts can be used to carry goods. The places passed through include Mashaojia and Hedong Wang Zaixi, namely Wanbaoshan. Wanbaoshan was still wasteland at that time and had not been opened up. However, Koreans were already secretly planting there. Wanbaoshan is under the jurisdiction of Changchun Prefecture. The mountain is not very high, just an earthen hill. If the canals are opened up and water from the Yitong River is introduced, it will become fertile land. The then magistrate of Changchun Prefecture was Zhang Luquan from Yin. Because of his fellow countryman, he allowed Wang Shangsan from Zhejiang to dig canals and plant 100,000 mu of land. In three years, he obtained 300,000 shi of grain. Unexpectedly, Wang was killed by Red Beards, and the land was abandoned. This is what Zhang Luquan, the magistrate of Changchun, told me. His words were full of regret. But when my boat passed Futian, I wanted to transport 100,000 telegraph poles to the riverbank and recruit laborers. Shandong people came to respond. During the gap in transporting the telegraph poles, I went to investigate the Wanbaoshan area. I only saw fields going east and west, and houses lined up. Listening to their language, seven out of ten people spoke in the Qi-Lu accent. The other three were Koreans. Their country had been destroyed, and they had no home to return to. They were employed by others, only seeking food. Only in my notes, I only knew that there were Zhangjiabao and Wangjiabao, but I did not know that it was Wanbaoshan.

At that time, I almost suspected that the Peach Blossom Spring was not a fable. These Koreans were all destroyed and lost their homes, their pain tearing at their livers. Like Wang Shangsan's digging and cultivation, he gathered Koreans, clothed them, and fed them, so he could gain their strength. Wang Shangsan was killed by bandits, and the land he cultivated was owned by the Qi-Lu people. The Qi-Lu people enslaved the Koreans, and resentment had accumulated for a long time. The Japanese were also good at giving small favors, lending them money to make them settle down to cultivate and support their families. Therefore, my transporting wood on the Yitong River was thirty years ago. The Japanese worked hard to build the South Manchuria Railway and devoted all their efforts to it. Unlike the Chinese government, which was large and bureaucratic, it never asked about the people. For example, Zhang Luquan, the magistrate of Changchun Prefecture, said to me, "Since Wang Shangsan died, all the cultivated land in Wanbaoshan has been abandoned." In fact, the Shandong people illegally cultivated without the approval of the government, which had already laid the root of today's fighting.

Hao Yongde rented Xiao Hanlin's wasteland and organized a rice field company. How could he grow rice without releasing the water from the Yitong River? Koreans sub-rented Hao Yongde's company, which was a private transfer. Originally, the water irrigation was mutually beneficial. The Koreans were strong, and the Japanese helped them. This is why the Shandong people were dissatisfied, resulting in this major fight.

Oh, Korean Children!

He Tianjian

Recently, it was reported that the Japanese drove Korean people to block our Yitong River and seize our Wanbaoshan fields. They also incited Korean people to burn and kill our overseas Chinese. I am indignant and write this.

There is a long whale in the East Sea, blinking its giant eyes.

It surges the sky's waves, sometimes competing with me.

China is my land, the Red County is my city.

Each has its own share of heaven, why forcibly annex it?

The Three Hans were originally my people, the beans and stalks were born together.

Suddenly the sacred artifact was lost, and they became barbarians.

They are innocent, and are made into fish and meat.

Black slaves have long been liberated, why are they still sacrificed?

My grief is not yet over, the cicada larvae are born.

They foolishly act as pioneers, becoming soldiers for others.

The Yitong blocks my water, and Wanbao stops my farming.

Still not satisfied, they drive the crowd to run away.

Hancheng staged burning and killing, a habitual skill of cutting off noses and tattooing faces.

Lu's blood splashed on Cai, the cold and heat have changed several times.

And now the flames are burning again, and ten thousand are used as fuel.

They claim to be protecting them, tigers and wolves leaning on each other.

Alas, my overseas Chinese, unarmed and unable to resist.

Their houses have been burned, and a group of villains are waiting outside the door.

Going in and out cannot avoid death, shaking the sky and shouting.

They are scattered for a while, and flesh and blood do not help each other.

How can I think about this time, life is as light as a feather.

Leaving the homeland for thousands of miles, a lonely person harmed in a foreign land.

Why do they dare to do this, diplomatic relations have been maintained for a long time.

Now it is the opposite, no different from throwing yourself into thorns.

Which country has no foreigners? Which country has no guests?

If the world is like this, how can the sun and moon be bright?

Tell the Korean children, how can you bear to kill your brothers?

Qingtan Records of the Xiyin Shuzhai (惜隂書齋清譚錄)

Ke Ding'an

Through the introduction of my dear friend Ma Mengrong, I met Mr. Xia Yizi from Jiangdu. Yesterday afternoon I went to visit. Mr. Xia was engaged in inkpad work, his hands were crimson. He quickly wiped them and came out to greet me, inviting me inside. I immediately felt a sense of antiquity and elegance, which made me envious. Mr. Xia has been studying inkpad for more than twenty years. The most valuable of its raw materials are: First, cinnabar, which is obtained from Yunnan and Guizhou, the so-called "Da Pi Sha" (大劈砂). As large as a longan, it is crystal clear like a gemstone when viewed under lamplight. Second, lotus silk, which is extracted from lotus roots and carefully refined before use. One qian of silk can only be extracted from one hundred catties of lake lotus. Its rarity can be seen. The use of lotus silk in inkpad is Mr. Xia's research achievement, which was unprecedented. It was first used in the finest inkpad because the cost is so high. Third, matured oil, which must be exposed to the sun and dew for dozens of winters and summers. What Mr. Xia uses has been treasured for fifteen years. Fourth, wild velvet, which is collected from the deep mountains and remote ridges of Sichuan Province, where people rarely go. It is soft and tough in texture, and then refined. All of these are not available on the market. Other ingredients, such as coral, agate, and pearls, must be carefully studied, with a balance of strictness and leniency, before success can be achieved. Being too hasty is like sand, while being too slow will cause it to not crack. Mr. Xia said that this work must be done personally. Once, a male worker said, "I would rather pull a cart all day than carefully grind for half a moment." Before he could reply, he had already run away. This is also a joke. Mr. Xia also said, "I have noticed that when calligraphers and painters create fan paintings, the seals they use are easily blurred unless they are dusted with pearl powder, which is not worthy of the exquisite works. I feel it is a pity. I have invented an inkpad that can dry immediately after being applied and cannot be wiped off. I plan to invite friends in the calligraphy and painting world to try it out." I was also treated to fine tea. The tea was picked from the highest peak of the Lion Peak, taking the tender leaves and making it with daffodil flowers. The water came from Huiquan and Hupao, and it was transported by a friend in Shaoxing wine jars that had not been used to hold wine. Mr. Xia is so fond of tea that he can be compared to Lu Yu and Lu Tong. Mr. Xia and I sat opposite each other, with a small table in the middle, on which were tea sets. He first poured water into a large teacup, took tea leaves and put them into the teapot. When the water temperature was right, he slowly poured it into the pot. After waiting a while, he shook the pot. Mr. Xia tasted it. It seemed that it was not yet ready. After another moment, we each poured a cup. As soon as I tasted it, the clear fragrance permeated my spleen. Mr. Xia said, "Drinking tea is a small matter, but there is a great principle in it. It is not just for quenching thirst. The water temperature must be just right, and the tea flavor must be mellow and harmonious. Then the sweetness will be long-lasting." After drinking four times, Mr. Xia said, "The taste is exhausted." There are still products made with plum blossoms, lotus flowers, etc., totaling more than thirty kinds. I will taste them with you in order. I said, "The phrase 'the fragrance lingers in the mouth and cheeks' can be used today." Mr. Xia smiled non-stop.

News from the Art World

Tao Shoubo, a famous calligrapher, painter, seal carver, has recently seen an increasing number of requests for calligraphy or painting on fans. He has set a price: 1 yuan for both sides of calligraphy and painting. An additional 10 cents for postage for out-of-town requests. Half a yuan per character for stone seals. Collection in five days. Samples are available. Enclose five cents for postage for mail requests. Send to the Shanghai Newspaper Office on Er Ma Road.

The Foreign Ministry Will Make a Second Representation Regarding the Korean Case 2

Demanding that Japan Take Real Responsibility

(Nanjing) Regarding the Korean massacre of overseas Chinese, after the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu arrives in Beijing tomorrow morning, the Foreign Ministry will make a second representation, demanding that Japan take real responsibility for this case and stating that China cannot be satisfied with the first reply. (14th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) A certain advisor said, "Since Japan acknowledges itself as the ruler of Korea, it cannot shirk responsibility for the Koreans' violence. Many people from various countries reside in Korea, and they will all feel insecure. Therefore, we hope that Japan will handle the aftermath properly." He also said, "Japan, facing political turmoil within its cabinet, wants to divert the nation's attention externally and incites Koreans to commit this atrocity. The tragic deaths of the overseas Chinese are no less than sacrifices to Japan's political turmoil. Is this not unjust?" From the perspective of international prestige and morality, Japan cannot shield the Koreans' criminal actions and must impose severe punishment. Furthermore, the officials responsible for maintaining public order in Korea should also be punished accordingly to uphold the spirit of their own laws. As for the right and wrong of the Wanpaoshan incident, it cannot be discussed together with the Korean case because the overseas Chinese in Korea were not involved in the Wanpaoshan incident." (14th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) A certain important figure in diplomatic circles said, "Japan insists on linking the Wanpaoshan case with the Korean incident, hoping to lightly evade its responsibility under international law. This clearly shows a lack of sincerity towards our protests. With so many Chinese compatriots killed and injured in Korea this time, Japan's responsibility is extremely clear. Yet, Japan still wants to shirk responsibility, only showing its unwillingness to be candid. The government will definitely not give up on this matter and must achieve the goals of compensation, punishing the murderers, issuing an apology, and guaranteeing that similar incidents will not happen again. As for the Wanpaoshan case, the government will also begin negotiations. Korean immigration has now reached over a million people, which has no basis in treaties. Legally speaking, this violates treaties for Japan and demonstrates leniency and negligence for China. However, how can this kind of negligence continue unchanged for so long? If Koreans follow the treaties, then their residence, travel, commerce, and cultivation in the Northeast should not be free. Behind the Wanpaoshan case, there was Japanese police leadership, giving people the feeling that wherever Koreans go, Japanese police follow. In short, unless Japan revises its laws, the fundamental problem of Koreans cannot be resolved." (14th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) After the Wanpaoshan incident occurred, the Foreign Ministry protested to Shigemitsu and the Japanese government. Shigemitsu recently formally replied, stating that he had not yet received official instructions and claiming that Korean authorities had prevented the tragedy and protected the overseas Chinese, attempting to evade responsibility. The Foreign Ministry immediately instructed the International Affairs and Asian Affairs Departments to draft a reply to refute this, which is expected to be sent out on the 15th. It is also reported that the Japanese government's reply will be brought by Shigemitsu on the 15th. (14th Central News Agency Dispatch)

The Hebei Provincial Party Headquarters Issues a Proclamation to Koreans 3

The Korean Ethnic Alliance Also Issues a Statement

(Beiping) The Hebei Provincial Party Headquarters sent a telegram to the National Government on the 13th, requesting serious

Page 4

negotiations regarding the Wanpaoshan case, punishment of the rioters who massacred overseas Chinese, and issued a proclamation to Koreans, stating that the Wanpaoshan incident was caused by a malicious plot and that Japanese imperialism is the common enemy. (14th Special Dispatch)

(Changsha) He Jian telegraphed the central government, urging serious steps to resolve both the Wanpaoshan and Korean cases. (14th Special Dispatch)

(Harbin) The Harbin National Diplomacy Support Association issued a proclamation to the public regarding the Wanpaoshan case, urging all sectors to unite against Japan. (14th Special Dispatch)

(Harbin) Today, various organizations held a joint meeting and decided: (1) to send representatives to comfort the overseas Chinese who suffered in Korea; (2) to send representatives to Wanpaoshan to comfort the farmers; (3) to send telegrams nationwide, requesting the government to urge serious diplomacy; (4) to raise 30,000 yuan as condolence money for the injured overseas Chinese in Korea. (14th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Korean Ethnic Alliance issued a statement, saying that China and Korea are two nations with the longest history, and now they are being used by others. Sima Zhao's intentions are obvious to everyone. Therefore, they issue a serious warning to the people of their own country, to seek ways to handle the aftermath well, and hope that Chinese compatriots will understand this difficulty. (14th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Nanjing Municipal Party Headquarters, considering that the Japanese and Korean rioters massacred overseas Chinese with extreme inhumanity, has ordered party headquarters in various districts to convene general membership meetings as soon as possible to discuss countermeasures. First, fixed propaganda teams will be dispatched as soon as possible to raise public awareness and unite in resistance, protecting overseas Chinese and avenging the shame. The Organization, Training, and Propaganda Departments, as well as the Civil Training Committee, will convene regular meetings to summon people from all walks of life and hold an anti-Japanese and overseas Chinese aid conference, convened by the Organization Department. (14th Special Dispatch)

Wang Rongbao Has Already Gone to Korea 4

Will the Former Governor-General Report the Truth?

(Tokyo) Ambassador Wang Rongbao, upon the order of his government, departed from Tokyo last night with the Chinese Consul in Kobe to Korea. He will contact Chinese consuls in various parts of Korea and the Governor-General's Office to conduct on-the-spot investigations and then go to Nanjing via Panyang and Beiping to report to Foreign Minister Wang. (14th Electrical Communication Dispatch)

(Tokyo) In today's cabinet meeting, the former Governor-General reported the truth and the amount of losses in the Korean incident as follows: After careful investigation of the Korean incident, it is known that there was no prior plan or ideological background. It was merely revenge for the Wanpaoshan incident. The estimated amount of losses: 103 Chinese dead, 75 seriously injured, 46 slightly injured; 2 Koreans dead, 70 police officers slightly injured. (14th Electrical Communication Dispatch)

Grain River Rice Market Gradually Tightens

Yesterday, two cars of Wan Ning passenger tip were loaded onto the Hu Ning Road, and the goods were piled in foreign warehouses. The sales disk has not yet opened.

South Market 15

Sources from all routes were scarce, and Pu Cun was also weak. Due to the cold and overcast weather, urban and rural store sales had more intention to enter, and the market felt even more clamorous. Therefore, the price of thick geng rose by another corner or so. The actual price of thin rice production was not small, and the arrival and accumulation were scarce. Not many customers bought it, but the market was lively, causing the price to continue to rise by one and a half chi. Zhong Su also followed slightly. Luyang tip was affected by the increasing amount of foreign rice, and sales were active, and the price was also tightened. The shape was firm, and the sales of Yin Hua goods were rare and promising, and the trend was stable. Due to major floods in various places, customers are moving to handle foreign rice, and local buyers are following suit, and market prices are rising.

Futures and Spot Wheat Prices Rise Gradually 16

In recent days, wheat prices have shown a firm and charming trend again. Although foreign wheat quotations continue to be small, three or four corners, the gold market has returned high, and exchange rates have shortened. Orderers cannot combine. Moreover, with continuous moldy rain, there is a risk of flooding in various places, and the low-lying farmland has already been flooded. Therefore, the inland gang's thoughts have turned firm again. Although buying is not very strong, the market has gradually become firmer. However, the local people are still lukewarm towards the factory's foreign wheat, which can be used in October, because the path of new wheat is very small. As a result, the price of this month rose by three cents compared to the previous week, August rose by three cents, September rose by four cents, and October, November, and December rose by five cents. In the spot wheat market, prices have become stable due to standard stability, and high-quality goods have been shouted up two or three cents. Medium and second-class goods are still flat. More than 4,000 packages of Kaitai, Dongtai, Wusong, Luodian, Penglai, Anting, Huangdu, Shuangfeng, and Wangxianqiao wheat were handled by Xinda, Huafeng, and Xiangxing.
