Automobile News

Special Article

Recent Overview of the British Automobile Industry 40

— Pei Gan

All industries in the world are declining. The automobile manufacturing industry has also been affected. A correspondent from a London newspaper recently provided an overview of the British automobile industry, as follows. Based on the facts, automobile manufacturers often display their new models at the automobile exhibition in mid-October. Therefore, to discuss the recent automobile industry, one must start from October. From October 1930 to March 1931, the number of newly registered automobiles was 74,184, a 3.1% decrease compared to the 76,550 registered during the same period last year. As of February 28, the total number of licensed automobiles was 839,262, a 4.3% increase compared to the 804,564 a year ago. As for gasoline consumption, whether it has decreased per car compared to before the commercial decline is uncertain, as there is no significant evidence. However, considering the recent rapid progress in small car manufacturing and the fuel efficiency of large cars, it can be asserted that the average mileage of each car is likely to increase. The automobile export industry shows few signs of decline. From October 1930 to April 1931, the number of British private cars exported totaled 12,600, compared to 18,037 in the previous year, a decrease of 20.2%. The markets in Ireland and South Africa have remained stable, while business in Australia has plummeted. The price of exported cars has fallen from £180 to £159 during the year. Simultaneously, imports have also decreased from 9,704 to 3,710. The average price of imported cars in April was £182, slightly higher than last year's £173.

Although there are no accurate figures for comparison with other countries outside of Britain, generally speaking, Britain's position is significantly more advantageous than its overseas competitors. British manufacturers' products account for 94% of the domestic market demand, compared to 87% a year ago. In other words, British manufacturers' products have decreased by approximately 2,300 units in the domestic market, while foreign exports have decreased by approximately 5,000 units. In reality, British industry has increased its sales by 2,500 units. The total number of cars sold in Britain (calculated by subtracting imports from domestic registrations and adding exports) from October to March totaled 81,912, a decrease compared to the previous year's 84,255. However, this loss is often offset by the decrease in imports. Considering the current situation, it is not bad. Britain's automobile exports are largest to Australia, especially in chassis exports. Therefore, the current economic difficulties in Australia have a significant impact on Britain. If Australia can overcome its obstacles, the British automobile industry will benefit significantly. The same applies to the political changes in India. The following table records the number of new registrations of private cars in Britain, including London, the Home Counties, Wales, Scotland, Northern Ireland, and other parts of England. The limited impact of the commercial decline on car registrations is noteworthy.

October 1930 to March 1931　October 1929 to March 1930　Percentage Decrease

London and the Home Counties　26,577 units　27,804 units　4.4

Wales, Scotland, and Northern Ireland　22,017 units　22,435 units　1.9

Other Parts of England　25,590 units　26,311 units　2.7

Total　74,184 units　76,550 units　3.1

Examining the horsepower categories of currently registered cars reveals a bright future for automobile manufacturers. Public preferences have also changed. Unfortunately, Britain, like a few other countries, does not publicly disclose statistics on automobile brand registrations. The 8-horsepower "baby car" still leads the way, with 20,139 new registrations from October to March, compared to 19,27 units in the previous year. This number demonstrates that 27% of current new car registrations are 8-horsepower small cars, while 17% of cars on the market are these small cars. Automobile manufacturers are making tireless efforts in manufacturing small cars. Prominent manufacturers such as Austin, Morris, Triumph, Singer, and Swift are producing many models, showing a trend towards simplification. A year ago, five prominent manufacturers produced a total of 23 models, while today they produce 28. Therefore, it may not be necessary for these manufacturers to face difficulties in lowering prices. Initially, due to Ford's plan to establish a new factory in Dagenham, with an annual production capacity of 50,000 cars for the British market, all manufacturers felt compelled to lower prices. 10-horsepower cars like Rover, Standard, and Swift are very popular and sell well. The number of new registrations this year is 8,167, compared to 4,743 a year ago. 12-horsepower cars, which were once popular, have now lost their position, with only 9,900 new registrations this year compared to 13,004 last year, a significant difference.

What is particularly noteworthy is that since the rise of the new Ford car, 15-horsepower cars like Morris, Armstrong-Siddeley, and Lagonda have seen slower sales and stagnation. The number of new registrations is 9,189, compared to 9,504 a year ago. The last three months have been particularly bleak. 16-horsepower cars like Austin, Crossley, Talbot, and Singer have also not fared well, with 8,816 new registrations compared to 9,197 sixteen years ago. Cars with more than 16 horsepower have suffered even greater blows, which is inevitable due to public economic constraints. The number of new registrations is 10,258, a 13.4% decrease compared to the previous year. However, there is still hope for the future of large cars. Although there is a current decline, they can maintain their position without further progress. Although the demand is not as strong as before, it is still relatively firm. The number of large car registrations is higher than that of imported American cars, indicating that there is still some hope for their future. Therefore, in summary, the decline in the automobile industry this year is less severe than in other industries. However, with Ford cars joining the price war next year, it is difficult to predict the future.

Another Advancement in Recent Automobile Engineering 41

— Huang Yingdai

Using High-Pressure Principles to Increase Driving Speed

The automobile has seen continuous improvements in its manufacturing aspect to this day, almost to the point of being brand new every day. Besides all kinds of improvements, recently there has been another great advancement, namely using high-pressure compression to increase speed and economize gasoline. The desire to use high-pressure principles in the automotive world has been around for a long time, but various obstacles were too numerous to overcome, and it could not be realized for a time. After almost thirty years of hard research in the automotive world, in recent years, various obstacles have finally been overcome, and the so-called high-pressure engine can finally meet us, which is a great advancement in automobile engineering. Speaking of today's automobiles, even touring cars use high-pressure engines. The height of the pressure, if compared with the cars of 1926, has already been exceeded by a lot. As for the so-called racing cars, they completely utilize high pressure, and their pressure exceeds that of touring cars by a lot more. Judging from the recent situation and thinking about the future, in the near future, the manufacturing method of racing cars will likely become completely different from that of touring cars. If this is not the case, then the engine will not be able to adapt to its racing environment.

The automobile is able to start depending on the power of gasoline, and the reason gasoline can produce power is due to the effect of pressure on the vapor produced by the gasoline before ignition. Today, the average pressure on each vehicle's gasoline vapor on the market is five times that of the past. As for racing cars, it is ten or eleven times that of the past. For this reason, racing cars can get a large amount of power per gallon of gasoline. This power can increase the driving speed. As for touring cars, the extra power gained through high compression not only increases speed, but also has a significant impact on things such as increased propulsion and gasoline economy. However, if we want to distribute the extra power gained in accordance with the law to various parts, and utilize it without waste, it is an extremely difficult task. Speaking of today's trends in the automotive world, gasoline economy is probably the biggest problem. Therefore, increasing the pressure only saves gasoline, and does not increase driving speed. Saving gasoline is probably the biggest problem. Therefore, increasing the pressure only saves gasoline, and does not increase driving speed. The reduction of power, the convenience of propulsion, and the increase of speed can all economize gasoline directly and indirectly.

The aforementioned manufacturing of automobiles, such as using high-pressure principles, can save gasoline, which has been proven by Mr. Miller, an expert in manufacturing racing cars for Rolls-Angeles. According to his statement, a tank of gasoline can increase the range by up to 130 miles, and this type of tank can hold 8 gallons of gasoline. Moreover, simply moving the head of the engine slightly can increase the pressure, and on the other hand, the range of the combustion chamber can also be reduced. The convenience of operation is really something that was not possible in the past. In addition, there is another significant proof, that is, a high-pressure car and an ordinary car are loaded with the same weight of goods, and driven on the same road for a distance of 150 miles. The driving results show that each gallon of the 8 gallons of gasoline can increase the driving range by more than 4 miles.

In addition, another automobile factory also uses a method to prove the effect of high pressure. At that time, a six-cylinder car was used, and the compression ratio was reduced from four to one, so the pressure of the gasoline vapor was only a quarter of the original. The driving range per gallon of gasoline was 20 miles, and the speed per hour was 26 miles. Then, the height of the compression was increased to six times the original. Other parts did not seem to be affected in any way, but the driving speed was greatly increased. The driving range per gallon of gasoline was 34 miles. Based on the above, it can be seen that increasing the compression can both increase speed and save gasoline. It is truly a win-win situation.

Translated and Compiled

Overseas News About Automobiles 42

— Song Yu

One Car for Every Four People: According to a survey by the American Automobile Drivers Association, there is now one car for every 4.6 people in the United States. This statistic is based on population census data. The total population in 1930 was 127,750,046. The total number of cars nationwide, including all 48 states and the District of Columbia, is 26,523,779 registered vehicles. This number includes passenger cars and trucks. California leads all states, with a ratio of one car for every 2.7 people. Alabama ranks last, with one car for every 9.5 people. New York is in the middle, with one car for every 5.4 people. The ratios for each state are as follows: Alabama 9.5, Arizona 3.9, Arkansas 8.4, California 2.7, Colorado 3.3, Connecticut 4.8, Delaware 4.2, District of Columbia 3.7, Florida 4.4, Georgia 8.5, Idaho 3.7, Illinois 4.6, Indiana 3.6, Iowa 3.1, Kansas 3.1, Kentucky 7.8, Louisiana 7.5, Maine 4.2, Maryland 5.0, Massachusetts 5, Michigan 3.6, Minnesota 3.4, Mississippi 8.4, Missouri 4.7, Montana, Nebraska 3.2, Nevada 3.0, New Hampshire 4.6, New Jersey 4.6, New Mexico 5.0, New York 5.4, North Carolina 6.9, North Dakota 5.7, Ohio 3.7, Oklahoma 4.5, Oregon 3.7, Pennsylvania 5.4, Rhode Island 5.0, South Carolina 7.9, South Dakota 3.3, Tennessee 7.1, Texas 4.2, Utah 4.4, Vermont 4.1, Virginia 6.4, Washington 3.5, West Virginia 6.4, Wisconsin 3.7, Wyoming 3.6.

Ford Factory Tours Various Cities: Ford Motor Company recently produced a sound film detailing the Ford car manufacturing process, assembly methods, and various manufacturing operations. It is being shown in cities, towns, and villages across the United States to provide those who have not visited the Ford factory with an understanding of car manufacturing. Because it is a sound film, watching it is like being in the factory itself. All aspects of the process, from smelting iron and casting steel to sawing wood and machining, can be seen in detail. It is both interesting and educational. Ford Motor Company produces thousands of cars daily, and the most crucial aspect of its manufacturing process is accuracy, ensuring that parts fit together perfectly during assembly. The film provides a detailed explanation of parts manufacturing and assembly, with no discrepancy, even in the slightest details. The film also shows all by-products of manufacturing. The planning and testing of these sound film tours have been underway for months, and the results have been remarkable. Therefore, multiple copies have been made to show in smaller towns. Additionally, various car accessories are displayed to complement the film.

Buick Cars Are Durable: According to a survey by Buick, many older Buick cars are still in common use. Some of these older cars date back to 1940, demonstrating their durability. Buick conducted a survey of car registrations in various counties in North America and found many older Buicks. Among the Buick cars in common use, 73,271 have been in use for ten years or more, and 2,500 have been in use for fifteen years or more. Approximately 115 have been in use for twenty years. Buick’s sales have been strong, with approximately 1.5 million Buick cars in use this year. With a total U.S. population of 122,000,000, one out of every eighty-one people drives a Buick. Considering families, one in every twenty households owns a Buick.

Two Million Cars This Year: Based on recent U.S. car sales figures, the outlook for car production and sales in 1931 is optimistic, and a new high record is expected. The profits of car companies are also expected to be the highest ever. Spring is usually the peak season for car sales. According to surveys, car sales across the U.S. in April showed no signs of decline. Based on this, the demand for cars in the summer is not expected to be significantly different. Given the strong demand this spring and summer, the sales for the entire year are expected to be quite impressive. Statisticians estimate that at least 2.5 million new cars are needed to replace old ones. However, even if only 2 million cars are sold, it would be quite satisfactory. Currently, the production and sales of Ford and Chevrolet cars have increased significantly compared to April. Ford estimates that over 125,000 cars will be produced in May, while Chevrolet expects to produce at least 110,000 six-cylinder cars.

Car Travel to Canada: Every summer, millions of Americans drive to Canada for travel. This summer, the estimated number of travelers is expected to be no less than 5.5 million. All these travelers will cross the international border into Canada. Most of the travelers come from California and the northern states. According to the Travel Department of the California Automobile Association, U.S. and Canadian customs officials at the Blaine, Washington border crossing will work around the clock, 24 hours a day, starting June 1st. Car travelers from the U.S. to Canada must present their state car registration certificates to pass the border; otherwise, they may face delays. Canadians exempt U.S. travelers staying in Canada for less than 90 days from all passport fees, tariffs, etc. Last year, 5,409,458 American cars entered Canada, of which 4,110,100 stayed in Canada for less than 24 hours. The number of cars entering Canada in 1930 increased by 900,649 compared to the previous year.

Ford Model A Unchanged: The rumors that Ford cars would undergo major changes have proven to be false. The Model A cars displayed at the annual car show in New York have been improved but not significantly altered. In addition to participating in the New York car show, Ford also holds its annual car show at 1710 Broadway. According to Ford representatives, Model A cars are being displayed at various car shows across the country for public viewing. Regarding reforms, apart from necessary improvements, not many changes will be made.

The Situation After the Opening of the Eastern Hubei Automobile Road 43

— Xueqian

The construction of automobile roads in Hubei Province has been underway for a long time. However, the actual opening to traffic has been quite difficult. This is because the labor required is significant, the funding is substantial, and the mileage is long. Therefore, although the construction has been carried out separately in the four regions of northern, southern, western, and eastern Hubei, the results have not fully met the plan. The recent opening of the Eastern Hubei Automobile Road to traffic, although only for a few months, has been appreciated by travelers and merchants for its convenience. However, since the opening to traffic is just beginning, the facilities are difficult to be comprehensive. Therefore, the gradual improvement in the future is expected from the officials concerned with road administration. Speaking of the situation after the opening of the Eastern Hubei Automobile Road, since the road has been opened to traffic, the car road traverses hundreds of miles in Huangpi, Huanggang, Macheng, and other counties, and can be reached in a few hours. The ticket price is also not very expensive. Compared with the pre-traffic period, it took three days to travel from Hankou to Macheng, and the travel expenses were more than ten yuan. The difficulty of traveling cannot be described in a word. Therefore, after the opening of traffic, passengers are quite crowded. The distance from Hankou to Macheng County is about two hundred Chinese miles, and the ticket price is more than four yuan. Buy a ticket and get on the bus at Sanyuanli, Hankou, at about 6 am. Pass through Qiaokou, Hengdian, Huangpi County, and Huanggang's Lijiaji, Macheng's Songbu Qiting Zhongguanyi, and reach Macheng County. There are more than a dozen stops of various sizes along the way. The bus stops at the big stations, and occasionally does not stop at the small stations, depending on the number of passengers on the bus. This is the situation of the bus. As for the types of buses, there are freight cars, passenger cars, long tickets, and short tickets. About a dozen buses run every day. It is said that the Eastern Hubei Automobile Road Bureau has more than 20 freight cars and passenger cars. At the beginning of the traffic, there was very little cargo and more passengers. Therefore, freight cars are not needed much, and passenger cars are quite insufficient. The Road Bureau then temporarily placed long benches in the car for use as passenger cars to meet temporary passengers and benefit merchants. The form of the freight car is the same as that of the freight car in Hankou City. The form of the passenger car is the same as that of the public bus in Hankou City, but it is slightly smaller and cleaner. There are five benches horizontally arranged on both sides of the car. Each bench can seat two people, and each car can seat 20 passengers. There is an iron fence on the roof for passengers to place their luggage and sundries at any time. The station sells tickets. Each car originally only sells 20 passenger tickets. However, there are many passengers, and they often reluctantly buy tickets and get on the bus after the limit is reached. Therefore, each passenger car often carries 25 or 26 passengers. Because of this, the car is extremely cramped. Although this is taken by the passengers themselves, if the ticket seller can never sell again after the limit of each car is reached, the order of 20 people per car can be maintained. However, at the beginning of the opening to traffic, there were often soldiers who refused to buy tickets and forcibly boarded the bus. Moreover, people who intercepted and boarded the bus halfway were also seen every day. Previously, the Construction Department sent a letter to the 13th Division Xia Douyin's department stationed on the route to patrol and protect at any time to ensure the safety of travelers. After stipulating the preferential example of official soldiers in full uniform and symbols riding for half price, such things are no longer common. This is the situation of the car type and ticket sales. In short, the road was initially built and is muddy. Therefore, every time after the rain, the mud is ankle-deep, and the car cannot travel. The bus cannot run after the rain. Even after the rain, when driving a car, the road is often rolled into wheel ruts that are several inches deep. The mud dries and hardens after the weather clears, and it is not easy to return to its original state for a while. Therefore, the car is bumpy and the head is dizzy, just like the public buses in Zhabei, Shanghai, that travel to Jiangwan. The situation is the same as the Eastern Hubei car road every time it rains. The Construction Department is now working hard to improve it and is designing and constructing it. It is planned to pave the road surface from Hankou to Macheng with coal lamps first, so that the water will leak after the rain and will not hinder traffic. This is the situation of the road surface. I also heard that recently, during the large-scale suppression of bandits, the road is to prevent bandits from posing as passengers and mixing into the car for other purposes. Therefore, great attention is also paid to the inspection of passengers. In addition to the inspection when buying tickets and boarding the bus, the troops stationed along the way also inspect at each station at any time. The Construction Department has sent Wu Fu to carry out inspections above Huangpi. Because the inspection is thorough, no major accidents have occurred since the opening of traffic, which is safer than other automobile roads. As for the ticket inspection, it is also very serious. If it is not a formal

Page 20

soldier riding in the car, even if he buys a preferential half-price ticket, he must make up the ticket when he is found at the destination station. This is the situation of the inspection and ticket supplement. Generally speaking, what this road urgently needs to improve at present is to add more passenger cars to facilitate travel. Because there are not enough passenger cars on this road, freight cars are often used as temporary substitutes. There are more than 40 passengers in the car, and at least 30 passengers. Although the freight car is slightly larger than the passenger car, the road surface is uneven, and the suffering of the bumps is even worse than that of the passenger car, which inevitably contains a lot of danger.

General Motors Sales Soar 46

— Fu

According to a report recently received by Mr. Mars, General Manager of the Shanghai General Motors Factory, General Motors' sales in the Americas and Canada accounted for 62% of the total number of cars in April of this year. If the sales in January, February, March and April are combined, they account for 50% of the total. According to last year's April figures, General Motors' sales accounted for 32%. Sales for the months of January, February, March and April last year accounted for approximately 35%. Compared with the two figures, the progress is obvious. It is commendable and enviable to have achieved such excellent results in a very short period of time. Most of the credit for this impressive performance should be attributed to the excellence of Chevrolet products. In total, the Chevrolet Company has more than 36,000 employees. Some of its factories have been working extra shifts since the fall of 1929 to catch up with the orders. In addition, the production of Buick, Oakland, and Pontiac cars has also increased. Sales of Oakland and Pontiac in April of this year increased by 40% compared to the previous month. This is the highest record since August 1929.

The overseas sales of various General Motors vehicles have also made significant progress. The total number of exports in April not only exceeded the previous month, but also doubled compared to the same month last year. It is especially noteworthy that the Yutoku Electric Railway Company in Japan used to carry passengers by electric train between Tokyo and Yutoku. Now, it has abolished the tracks and electric trains and replaced them with Chevrolet buses. This is sufficient evidence of the superior quality and excellence of Chevrolet products, and the reason for their ever-increasing sales.

New News from the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau 47

— Fan

Highway Bureau Renamed Management Bureau, Vehicle Increases Implemented in Stages, Construction Plan Temporarily Suspended

Zhejiang Province is a national leader in road construction and traffic. Since the establishment of the Provincial Road Bureau in the 11th year of the Republic of China (1922), it has been committed to planning and building highways. In the 16th year of the Republic of China (1927), the National Government moved its capital to Nanjing, and each province established a Construction Department. The Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department, recognizing the importance of highways, reorganized the Provincial Road Bureau into the Highway Bureau in April of the 17th year of the Republic of China (1928), expanded its organization, actively carried out its work, and formulated a major provincial road network plan and a five-year construction plan, which were implemented in stages. Priority was given to the construction of main lines. The budget for this year included the addition of 149 vehicles, the construction of the entire Shaoxing-Wenling line road surface, the Qiantang River highway bridge, and two Oujiang-Lingjiang bridges, increasing the total mileage to 1,300 kilometers. The shortage of funds amounted to more than 2.63 million yuan, which was paid by the provincial treasury. The highway construction plan has achieved considerable success today.

Since the reorganization of the provincial government, Chairman Zhang Xian, in view of the large amount of government expenses in Zhejiang Province, which were insufficient to cover expenditures, compiled a new budget and implemented a austerity policy. Health and construction projects that had already been successful were merged and suspended one after another. The Highway Bureau was affected by this and has been reduced in size several times. However, due to the financial difficulties, it was difficult to maintain. Therefore, after the 400th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, it was decided to rename the Highway Bureau as the Highway Management Bureau, which would specialize in road maintenance. Vehicles would be increased in stages, and all plans and roads under construction would be temporarily suspended until the provincial treasury had surplus funds to handle them again.

The original route set by Zhejiang Province was more than 10,000 li, and only one-fifth of it has been built. Now, with the reorganization due to the austerity policy, the development of highways in the future may not be as rapid as in the past.

Recent Situation of Roads in Guangzhou City 48

— Junchao

The Guangzhou Municipal Bureau of Public Works has been sparing no effort in planning and building roads in the city recently. The following routes have now been planned and are being constructed in order:

(1) Sansheng Society Road: The route of Sansheng Society Road starts from Fengyuan Sandbank in Fengyuan Street, passes through Shilou Enzhou Straight Street, and ends at Sansheng Heng Lane on Sansheng Main Street. This road is the most important trunk road in Xiguan. The plan and materials have also been specified. The road surface is 60 feet wide and 5 inches high. The sidewalks on both sides are 12 feet wide. The engineering cost of the road is 97,500 yuan. The engineering cost of bridges and culverts is 45,000 yuan. The compensation for private property and relocation costs 50,000 yuan. The external expenses are 3,000 yuan. The total expenditure is 195,500 yuan. The road fee collected is 213,711 yuan, one dime and two copper coins. The income and expenditure ratio has a balance of 18,211 yuan, one dime and two copper coins. This money will be used to improve the road surface. The entire road plan has been decided by the Municipal Executive Meeting and will be constructed at the end of August of this year. (2) North Straight Street Road: The construction of Zhonghua Road in the city was originally divided into three sections. The southern section is Xiaoshi Street. The middle section is Sipailou. The northern section is North Straight Street. The construction of the southern and middle sections has been completed long ago. However, the northern section has not yet started. The route starts from Huiqing West Street, passes through Dade Straight Street, crosses Dexuan West Road, and ends at the intersection of the old Beida City Gate, connecting Xicun Highway, Panfu Road, and Zhenhailou Road. The entire line is 3,700 feet long and is also one of the important trunk roads. Bids are now being invited and construction can start in one month. (3) Dexing South Road: The Dexing South Road from Xidi Second Road to Xidi Main Road has long been measured and is ready for construction. However, the width of the road is slightly narrow. Therefore, the merchants and residents of the road recently jointly requested the municipal government to order the bureau to build the road in accordance with the width of ordinary roads in order to facilitate traffic. The municipal government therefore ordered the Bureau of Public Works to investigate and reply so that construction can begin immediately. (4) Xihu Street Road: This road starts from Xihu Street, passes through Dayoucang Road to Weixin Road and Guanlian Street, and reaches Jiaoyu Road. (5) Renji Main Street Road: This road starts from Renji Main Street and reaches Haizhu Road. The plans for all the above roads have been completed and will be constructed soon.

(1) Xianhao Street Road (2) Zhoutouzui East Street (3) Laolong Street Road (4) Yuanhe Tongjin Road (5) Baoyuan Ninth Street to Fengyuan East Street Road (6) Baiyun Mountain to Guangfan Flower Road: The above roads are in urgent need of planning.

(1) Jiuxin Street Road (2) Youlanmen to Banxiang Lane Road (3) Suoyi Street to Huangsha Road (4) Haiqiu New Embankment Road (5) Penglai New Street to Guangdong Road Factory Road (6) Second Pu to Fifth Pu and Xihe Road (7) Eleventh Pu to Mibu Road (8) Guanmin Market to Xicun Pingdan Road (9) Eleventh Pu to Duobao South Road (10) Ronghua West Twelfth Pu Road (11) Dongshan Qian Street to Eshi Liao Shahe Road (12) Yuexiu South to Dongshan Zilai Street Road (13) Wenchang Lane to Shanglongjin Road (14) Wuxian Straight Zengsha Nan Huilongli Road: The above roads are all under construction. Guangzhou, after the completion of each road, its municipal administration will surely become a model for the country.

Social News

Chinese Braided Elastic Fabric Industry Presents Significant Progress 50

Observations from the Japanese Side

According to the Eastern Daily News, an article submitted by Sotomi Tetsujiro, the chairman of the Japan Braided Elastic Fabric Industry Association, states that the Chinese braided elastic fabric industry has recently shown significant progress and development. Six years ago, there were only five companies in Shanghai organized as braided elastic fabric factories. According to a survey last year, the number of company-organized factories has reached 41, with an investment of 1,575,600 yuan and 6,536 workers. Furthermore, factories are also being added in Tianjin, Hong Kong, Wuxi, and other places. As for the amount of braided elastic fabric exported from Shanghai, it was 231,872 dozen four years ago, and it increased to 421,928 dozen last year, approximately doubling. The sales route of Chinese exported braided elastic fabric is also in Southeast Asia and India, which are the main sales routes for Japanese exported braided elastic fabric. The Japanese exported braided elastic fabric industry feels quite threatened by this. Furthermore, an investigation into the reasons for the development of the Chinese braided elastic fabric industry shows that (1) the prices of raw materials, cotton and cotton yarn, are relatively low; (2) manufacturing labor costs are low. In addition, there are three strategies for the Japanese exported cotton product industry to counter the Chinese cotton product industry: (1) abolition of cotton yarn tariffs; (2) granting of bonded factories; (3) suppression of work shortening.

The United States Establishes New Maritime Transport Policy 51

Sets Up Ten Committees

New York News: Since the European War, the United States Shipping Board has adopted the principle of "American goods in American ships," aiming in principle to have American ships carry more than 50% of American goods. According to a recent survey, only 47% of imported goods and 32% of exported goods are carried by American ships, far from the goal. Because the Shipping Board wants to establish a maritime transport policy, it has established ten committees, including the American Goods in American Ships Committee, the Fast Ship Postage Investigation Committee, and the Foreign Trade Investigation Committee, and ordered them to submit investigation reports separately by July 1. It intends to establish a new maritime transport policy based on this and submit a proposal to the next Congress. It believes that after President Hoover's international debt proposal is realized, the economy will gradually transform and the movement of world materials will increase, so it hopes to thoroughly implement the principle of "American goods in American ships."

Large Airship Carrying 50 Passengers 52

Manufactured in the United Kingdom, to be Completed Next Spring

London News: The United Kingdom is currently manufacturing a large transoceanic airship made entirely of stainless steel. A sealed bridge is set up between the cabin and the cockpit, and the pilot can regularly travel back and forth between the cabin. Its passenger seats are set up in five cabins and can accommodate 50 passengers. The cabin equipment is quite sophisticated. The engine is equipped with six Rolls-Royce engines, which can produce 5,400 horsepower. The maximum speed is 144 miles per hour, and the average speed is 120 miles per hour. When carrying 40 passengers, the range is 1,000 miles. When carrying 12 passengers, the range is 2,300 miles. The airship is scheduled to be completed next spring.

Japanese Rayon Fabric Imports Greatly Reduced 53

Due to the Impact of Italian Goods and Low Silver Prices

Tokyo News: Japanese rayon fabric exports have increased in quantity due to falling prices. The export volume from January to May was 49,558,000 square yards, worth 14,633,000 yuan. Compared with the same period last year, the price decreased by 11,053,000 yuan and the quantity increased by 14,143,000 square yards. Among them, the export volume to China from January to May was 413,000 square yards, worth 168,000 yuan. In the same period last year, the volume was 989,000 square yards, worth 568,000 yuan. This is because the impact of Italian products and the decline in silver prices have significantly reduced exports.

International Linguistics Conference to Be Held Next Month 54

Discussing Matters Such as the Organization of Research Institutions

Geneva Dispatch: The Second International Linguistics Conference is scheduled to be held in Geneva in August of this year. The conference will bring together prominent figures in phonetics and grammar from around the world to discuss the organization of language research institutions, the standardization of linguistic terminology, the standardization of phonetic symbols, the relationship between the true value of language and phonology, the study of dialects, the development of language, the practical value of artificial languages in the future, the publication of studies belonging to the Indo-Germanic language family, and the publication of studies belonging to other language families, and other related matters.

Guidelines for Social News Submissions 55

(1) Articles should concern domestic and international science, industry, commerce, or rural affairs.

(2) News related to hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life is welcome. Illustrations are limited to lyrical paintings of various aspects of social life.

(3) Photographs of seasonal events, landscapes, flora and fauna, people, and news-related photography are acceptable. Photographs of women in seasonal or scenic settings are especially welcome.

(4) The length of each article should not exceed 2,000 characters.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write horizontally; avoid sloppy handwriting. Western language should be minimized. If the original text must be quoted, it should be appended below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink for illustrations, and do not use colored paper. Use black ink on white paper.

(8) Please indicate "Social News Editor" for incoming manuscripts.

(9) All submissions will not be returned, whether published or not. If a return is required, it must be stated in advance and sufficient postage must be attached.

(10) Payment for articles is in three tiers: $3, $2, and $1 per thousand characters. Illustrations, special drawings, and photographs will be compensated separately according to the same example.
